-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="4bc409213d7545eba32f9fd86ae8dfb9">**`Destructuring Syntax`**<span offset-key="4bc409213d7545eba32f9fd86ae8dfb9:1"> : Allows you to extract parts of an array or obj intro distinct variables.</span></span>

## 

<span key="574693557c23490db1c13a4d5c5d0db8">**Destructuring Parameters**</span>

<span key="b5fdab1b8a4e4ed9bfb4ed80a111988d"><span offset-key="b5fdab1b8a4e4ed9bfb4ed80a111988d:0">We can also destructure </span>**incoming parameters**<span offset-key="b5fdab1b8a4e4ed9bfb4ed80a111988d:2"> of a function. This is very useful when we're passing objects around to different functions.</span></span>

## 

<span key="9118b6f6f3334ceab97fd527c5026619"><span offset-key="9118b6f6f3334ceab97fd527c5026619:0">Plain Old JS Object Lesson Concepts (W2D2) - Concepts</span></span>

1.  <span class="r-1awozwy r-1nf4jbm r-6koalj r-18u37iz r-gg6oyi r-ubezar r-16dba41 r-135wba7 r-1m04atk r-1pyaxff" contenteditable="false" style="height:24px">1.</span>
    <span key="28bdc51b900e4fe69b80e1778deaf3cf"><span offset-key="28bdc51b900e4fe69b80e1778deaf3cf:0">Label variables as either Primitive vs. Reference</span></span>

    <span key="a1601d52764c48258af4ddcfd5999009"><span offset-key="a1601d52764c48258af4ddcfd5999009:0">There are 5 primitive data types:</span></span>

    <span key="470b262afddd4a24b9c78e26b1ba3946"><span offset-key="470b262afddd4a24b9c78e26b1ba3946:0">Boolean, Null, Undefined, Number, String</span></span>

    <span key="7b97fa5e3cdb4da4b8d702c376f4d8df"><span offset-key="7b97fa5e3cdb4da4b8d702c376f4d8df:0">1 Reference Type:</span></span>

    <span key="5f3802b3f158432483a8f148438dc7af"><span offset-key="5f3802b3f158432483a8f148438dc7af:0">Object (arrays are a kind of object)</span></span>

2.  <span class="r-1awozwy r-1nf4jbm r-6koalj r-18u37iz r-gg6oyi r-ubezar r-16dba41 r-135wba7 r-1m04atk r-1pyaxff" contenteditable="false" style="height:24px">2.</span>
    <span key="84918fcd9c7d4292a8c5ed352deba313"><span offset-key="84918fcd9c7d4292a8c5ed352deba313:0">Identify when to use . vs \[\] when accessing values of an object:</span></span>

<span key="85f8ce73fd5b40fdb480c5e47221956b">**Notes**</span>

## 

<span key="c4742f40c3944993b311accb35d71067">**Callbacks: Using a Function as an Argument**</span>

<span key="b2de10ef516d48a5bf2f835310b186c5">**What is a callback?**</span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="6c6ea3769fec45c1b5d2dac80c109358"><span offset-key="6c6ea3769fec45c1b5d2dac80c109358:0">A </span>**`callback`**<span offset-key="6c6ea3769fec45c1b5d2dac80c109358:2"> is always a function that is being passed into another function.</span></span>

1

<span key="22c0a7e4fca94d6caff0c41d35bf5636"><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="22c0a7e4fca94d6caff0c41d35bf5636:0">let</span><span offset-key="22c0a7e4fca94d6caff0c41d35bf5636:1"> </span><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="22c0a7e4fca94d6caff0c41d35bf5636:2">foobar</span><span offset-key="22c0a7e4fca94d6caff0c41d35bf5636:3"> </span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="22c0a7e4fca94d6caff0c41d35bf5636:4">=</span><span offset-key="22c0a7e4fca94d6caff0c41d35bf5636:5"> </span><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="22c0a7e4fca94d6caff0c41d35bf5636:6">function</span><span offset-key="22c0a7e4fca94d6caff0c41d35bf5636:7"> </span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="22c0a7e4fca94d6caff0c41d35bf5636:8">(</span><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="22c0a7e4fca94d6caff0c41d35bf5636:9">callback</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="22c0a7e4fca94d6caff0c41d35bf5636:10">)</span><span offset-key="22c0a7e4fca94d6caff0c41d35bf5636:11"> </span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="22c0a7e4fca94d6caff0c41d35bf5636:12">{</span></span>

    <span key="7ed34199e3cd4d77acf5f6fc65656913">**`Anonymous Callback`**<span offset-key="7ed34199e3cd4d77acf5f6fc65656913:1"> : When we use a function expression directly.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="642b671a92c34bad84b447f2bb8f1676"><span offset-key="642b671a92c34bad84b447f2bb8f1676:0">Typically we want to assign our callback to a name if we plan on using it multiple times, an anonymous callball is better if it's just single use.</span></span>

    <span key="4cffb02d18cc407cae906eb2c61639ba">**`Math.sqrt`**<span offset-key="4cffb02d18cc407cae906eb2c61639ba:1"> built in function being passed directly in as an argument.</span></span>

<span key="8b388948677c4846ae27b4ca4d7528b5">**Refactoring for an Optional Callback**</span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="e37740a62a134eaa8bbe11f6930dc9a1"><span offset-key="e37740a62a134eaa8bbe11f6930dc9a1:0">We can add in a conditional to make the callback optional. (This is a very common pattern in Javascript!)</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC03MjczN18iIGNsYXNzPSJyLWg3Z2RvYiByLTEwcHR1bjcgci0xdnppOHhpIiBzdHlsZT0id2lkdGg6MTZweCI+PHBhdGggZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBjbGlwLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGQ9Ik0wIC41QS41LjUgMCAwMS41IDBoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNVY0aC0xVjFIMXY5aDN2MUguNWEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUtLjVWLjV6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTUgNS41YS41LjUgMCAwMS41LS41aDEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS41LjV2MTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LjVoLTEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNXYtMTB6TTYgNnY5aDlWNkg2eiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

## 

<span key="2f88820fd9734a9ba81ab8b7a12dd3cb">**Callback Functions as First Class Objects**</span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="efa20963dcf34723af14dc088a369045">**`First-Class Object`**<span offset-key="efa20963dcf34723af14dc088a369045:1"> : A type that supports the same basic operations as most other types. (i.e. Numbers, Strings & Booleans)</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="0defb36d768e44bca579d31bda86c982"><span offset-key="0defb36d768e44bca579d31bda86c982:0">First-Class Objects must be able to do </span>**three things**<span offset-key="0defb36d768e44bca579d31bda86c982:2">:</span></span>

    -   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

        <span key="6befdb5b2f5542d79694ead74c061873"><span offset-key="6befdb5b2f5542d79694ead74c061873:0">They can be stored in variables.</span></span>

        -   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

            <span key="032652ad4e714fc4927528b6ab85adb3"><span offset-key="032652ad4e714fc4927528b6ab85adb3:0">Function Expression Notation.</span></span>

    -   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

        <span key="3bb27c05b1444305a41ee727a3673e64"><span offset-key="3bb27c05b1444305a41ee727a3673e64:0">They can be passed as arguments.</span></span>

        -   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

            <span key="70a5c6ed589646c5a02bd39b98cd6ecb"><span offset-key="70a5c6ed589646c5a02bd39b98cd6ecb:0">Callback Functions.</span></span>

    -   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

        <span key="139dab4749984fe995ea85d21f1f677f"><span offset-key="139dab4749984fe995ea85d21f1f677f:0">They can be returned in functions.</span></span>

        1

        <span key="b081115fc5f241599b0c0b71881ca3f0"><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="b081115fc5f241599b0c0b71881ca3f0:0">function</span><span offset-key="b081115fc5f241599b0c0b71881ca3f0:1"> </span><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="b081115fc5f241599b0c0b71881ca3f0:2">foo</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="b081115fc5f241599b0c0b71881ca3f0:3">()</span><span offset-key="b081115fc5f241599b0c0b71881ca3f0:4"> </span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="b081115fc5f241599b0c0b71881ca3f0:5">{</span></span>

        2

    <span key="79c51da977c846d896e1534aa4af5447"><span offset-key="79c51da977c846d896e1534aa4af5447:0">As we have just proved above, functions are indeed first-class objects!</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="84f7d132431a4dcab09d624e917e206c">**`Higher-Order Function`**<span offset-key="84f7d132431a4dcab09d624e917e206c:1"> : A function that should either accept another function as an argument, or return a function as an output.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="c487a61a7c8140339abb500885506772"><span offset-key="c487a61a7c8140339abb500885506772:0">Callback Functions are passed into Higher-Order Functions.</span></span>

# 

<span key="f470311adbd5480b8e62d7873ab5d43c">**Notes**</span>

## 

<span key="dc048d107c5842d6b250b48f18dfc85b">**All About Scope in Javscript**</span>

<span key="e2591cb895e440fa8c03999a1f705c03"><span offset-key="e2591cb895e440fa8c03999a1f705c03:0">The </span>**`scope`**<span offset-key="e2591cb895e440fa8c03999a1f705c03:2"> of a program in JS is the set of variables that are available for use within the program.</span></span>

<span key="03c7024b65814d8facdf9ca78b557267">**Advantages of utilizing scope**</span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="7d0958294a204d6f9cf6baf3e389a2c4">**`Security`**<span offset-key="7d0958294a204d6f9cf6baf3e389a2c4:1"> : Adds security by ensuring variables can only be access by pre-defined parts of our program.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="b96dd15f1f354d44af1621333d0d9fa6">**`Reduced Variable Name Collisions`**<span offset-key="b96dd15f1f354d44af1621333d0d9fa6:1"> : Restricts re-using variable names; helps prevent overwriting variable names.</span></span>

<span key="06a3f8ae5762488bafbe9a1d6f1ceec7">**Different Kinds of Scope**</span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="523571ca738246b3a2031227f58a846e">**`Global Scope`**</span>

    -   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

        <span key="e8f62b56b79643ef97c9ec9c107fa486"><span offset-key="e8f62b56b79643ef97c9ec9c107fa486:0">The widest and outermost scope.</span></span>

    -   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

        <span key="26963addf32e46038024a3bb744155c6"><span offset-key="26963addf32e46038024a3bb744155c6:0">Represented by the </span>**`window`**<span offset-key="26963addf32e46038024a3bb744155c6:2"> obj in the browser and the </span>**`global`**<span offset-key="26963addf32e46038024a3bb744155c6:4"> obj in Node.js.</span></span>

    -   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

        <span key="73653d148d0a40a488ab498a729b69fa"><span offset-key="73653d148d0a40a488ab498a729b69fa:0">Try to avoid these as much as possible.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="f2eede611b4e4a7d969f9aa584486a52">**`Local Scope`**</span>

    -   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

        <span key="8eecd7da1dd14b8f9410e6916a87462e"><span offset-key="8eecd7da1dd14b8f9410e6916a87462e:0">Scope within a function.</span></span>

    -   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

        <span key="adf60464ef6145089af891807f948640"><span offset-key="adf60464ef6145089af891807f948640:0">Includes function arguments, variables declared within function, also </span>**any variables already declared when the function was defined**</span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="2276801044de4ba99dbbb3823df5eb42">**`Block Scope`**</span>

    -   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

        <span key="bbdf36c2e24e47b598a604cfcdd56fb0"><span offset-key="bbdf36c2e24e47b598a604cfcdd56fb0:0">Contents within curly braces.</span></span>

<span key="16f1dd2c61fa4c0388dfa59b49ca2a8e">**Scope Chaining: Variables and Scope**</span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC03MjczN18iIGNsYXNzPSJyLWg3Z2RvYiByLTEwcHR1bjcgci0xdnppOHhpIiBzdHlsZT0id2lkdGg6MTZweCI+PHBhdGggZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBjbGlwLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGQ9Ik0wIC41QS41LjUgMCAwMS41IDBoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNVY0aC0xVjFIMXY5aDN2MUguNWEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUtLjVWLjV6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTUgNS41YS41LjUgMCAwMS41LS41aDEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS41LjV2MTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LjVoLTEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNXYtMTB6TTYgNnY5aDlWNkg2eiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="fd7552697b674c53a27a7d91830b293f"><span offset-key="fd7552697b674c53a27a7d91830b293f:0">A key scoping rule is that an inner scope </span>**does**<span offset-key="fd7552697b674c53a27a7d91830b293f:2"> have access to variables in the outer scope.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="6863679aa9f649ffbf9aeb74c016d79f">**`Scope Chaining`**<span offset-key="6863679aa9f649ffbf9aeb74c016d79f:1"> : When a variable is not found within the immediate scope, JS will keep searching outwards until it matches the one we are referencing.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="9a13945e48a842d9bebfb54991dbb56b"><span offset-key="9a13945e48a842d9bebfb54991dbb56b:0">Important to note while inner scopes can search outwards, outer scopes cannot reference inner variables!</span></span>

<span key="6288d189303142d5852077dcc7254436">**Lexical Scope**</span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="302920caea824b949f8700055c716eb3">**`Lexing Time`**<span offset-key="302920caea824b949f8700055c716eb3:1"> : When you run a piece of JS code that is parsed before it is run.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="a0bf6d50bef74079b3e896287e36d42a"><span offset-key="a0bf6d50bef74079b3e896287e36d42a:0">JS language does not have dynamic scope.</span></span>

## 

<span key="852109ecdc014deea359fab92967617e">**Different Variables in Javascript**</span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="9d78eac027bc4d31b51d9df96eb4512c">*A variable always evaluates to the value it contains no matter how you declare it.*</span>

<span key="5e5c5e260ba5402b8f381ba90d830c48">**The different ways to declare variables**</span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="06e72cdf07914652b0c61240df8f9180">**`let`**<span offset-key="06e72cdf07914652b0c61240df8f9180:1"> : can be re-assigned; block-scoped.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="c7c8c0617d6b4c1fb36983ad82b29888">**`const`**<span offset-key="c7c8c0617d6b4c1fb36983ad82b29888:1"> : no re-assignment; block scoped.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="56f894c7406246b09426e2422ad9aa66">**`var`**<span offset-key="56f894c7406246b09426e2422ad9aa66:1"> : May or may not be re-assigned; scoped to a function.</span></span>

<span key="d06fd8938701400abad96d39dd1f3eab">**Hoisting and Scoping with Variables**</span>

<span key="1d592e5c947444b4ab5714fe24da5dfb">**`Hoisting`**<span offset-key="1d592e5c947444b4ab5714fe24da5dfb:1"> is a JavaScript mechanism where variables and function declarations are moved to the top of their scope before code execution.</span></span>

<span key="448150bf24004a48bdb12abe44c0f32f">**Function-Scoped Variables**</span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="ffc74ee709b14261ad95fb8dd76a44d7"><span offset-key="ffc74ee709b14261ad95fb8dd76a44d7:0">As we learned, var creates function-scoped variables, this means our declared var keyword variable will be confined to the scope of our current function.</span></span>

<span key="931a419c11d242f0839ef260b04313f3">**Hoisting with function-scoped variables**</span>

1

<span key="1c96bdb34a814bedb9023d337ffd8209"><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="1c96bdb34a814bedb9023d337ffd8209:0">function</span><span offset-key="1c96bdb34a814bedb9023d337ffd8209:1"> </span><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="1c96bdb34a814bedb9023d337ffd8209:2">test</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="1c96bdb34a814bedb9023d337ffd8209:3">()</span><span offset-key="1c96bdb34a814bedb9023d337ffd8209:4"> </span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="1c96bdb34a814bedb9023d337ffd8209:5">{</span></span>

2

<span key="a88edd65ad5246f8952c93050c51dca1"><span offset-key="a88edd65ad5246f8952c93050c51dca1:0"> </span><span class="r-17y197c" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="a88edd65ad5246f8952c93050c51dca1:1">// var hoistedVar;</span></span>

3

<span key="f02f525e5f0d432d8ecf0951e80253ca"><span offset-key="f02f525e5f0d432d8ecf0951e80253ca:0"> console</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="f02f525e5f0d432d8ecf0951e80253ca:1">.</span><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="f02f525e5f0d432d8ecf0951e80253ca:2">log</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="f02f525e5f0d432d8ecf0951e80253ca:3">(</span><span offset-key="f02f525e5f0d432d8ecf0951e80253ca:4">hoistedVar</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="f02f525e5f0d432d8ecf0951e80253ca:5">);</span><span offset-key="f02f525e5f0d432d8ecf0951e80253ca:6"> </span><span class="r-17y197c" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="f02f525e5f0d432d8ecf0951e80253ca:7">// => undefined</span></span>

4

<span key="df10474e03f54ffbb41e1de3dd1359e5"><span offset-key="df10474e03f54ffbb41e1de3dd1359e5:0"> </span><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="df10474e03f54ffbb41e1de3dd1359e5:1">var</span><span offset-key="df10474e03f54ffbb41e1de3dd1359e5:2"> hoistedVar </span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="df10474e03f54ffbb41e1de3dd1359e5:3">=</span><span offset-key="df10474e03f54ffbb41e1de3dd1359e5:4"> </span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="df10474e03f54ffbb41e1de3dd1359e5:5">10</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="df10474e03f54ffbb41e1de3dd1359e5:6">;</span></span>

5

<span key="08bef61d88f440129222cb0627c20e77"><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="08bef61d88f440129222cb0627c20e77:0">}</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC03MjczN18iIGNsYXNzPSJyLWg3Z2RvYiByLTEwcHR1bjcgci0xdnppOHhpIiBzdHlsZT0id2lkdGg6MTZweCI+PHBhdGggZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBjbGlwLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGQ9Ik0wIC41QS41LjUgMCAwMS41IDBoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNVY0aC0xVjFIMXY5aDN2MUguNWEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUtLjVWLjV6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTUgNS41YS41LjUgMCAwMS41LS41aDEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS41LjV2MTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LjVoLTEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNXYtMTB6TTYgNnY5aDlWNkg2eiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="39fd432298624f56afc7faeb4195cd22"><span offset-key="39fd432298624f56afc7faeb4195cd22:0">Even though we initially declared & initizalized our variable underneath the console.log var variables are "hoisted" to the top, but only in declaration.</span></span>

<span key="97b4cb1f42554013a60f167d3a8e0ef2">**Block-Scoped Variables**</span>

<span key="c9518543c43f4e4f8c22b871539b11b2"><span offset-key="c9518543c43f4e4f8c22b871539b11b2:0">Things that create block-scopes:</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="6d34e4d66aeb4831908b7e58907dd552"><span offset-key="6d34e4d66aeb4831908b7e58907dd552:0">If Statements</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="3002c7df09344e788c2d24ec5470b756"><span offset-key="3002c7df09344e788c2d24ec5470b756:0">While Loops</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="a3cf631a52b047fc85541e3666865112"><span offset-key="a3cf631a52b047fc85541e3666865112:0">Switch Statements</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="3b4ca907fd224471993cc4d6ea6b1be6"><span offset-key="3b4ca907fd224471993cc4d6ea6b1be6:0">For Loops</span></span>

<span key="d11ab38edae64d5e9fd6570abe17576f">**Properties of Constants**</span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="68ca84f4e8894b0baccaf42831668d6f"><span offset-key="68ca84f4e8894b0baccaf42831668d6f:0">They are block-scoped like let.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="ec4adc1f71cf4bc0935e9c5252c46587"><span offset-key="ec4adc1f71cf4bc0935e9c5252c46587:0">JS will enforce constants by raising an error if you try to change them.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="72a0ac0e91af4e169c24a90e0c6ebb4f"><span offset-key="72a0ac0e91af4e169c24a90e0c6ebb4f:0">Constants that are assigned to Reference Types are </span>**mutable**</span>

<span key="4ad73271d1834bcb99e62c902d02f50f">**Hoisting with block-scoped variables**</span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="21c44cfc0fa9440f85cdc53918129c6f"><span offset-key="21c44cfc0fa9440f85cdc53918129c6f:0">Unlike vars in function scopes, let and const in their block scopes do not get their declarations hoisted.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="a050b3bc3a814bf8935a01dca6efaf2d"><span offset-key="a050b3bc3a814bf8935a01dca6efaf2d:0">Instead they are not initalized until their definitions are evaluated - instead of undefined we will get an error.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="23bd581e02ed4ec2bf2ce42764fa6e15">**`Temporal Dead Zone`**<span offset-key="23bd581e02ed4ec2bf2ce42764fa6e15:1"> : The time before a let or const variable is declared.</span></span>

<span key="cc63387b3cd642e9a2cf0913a4e4034c">**Function Scope vs Block Scope**</span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="4f021a9cc2b548248fa2bba736f267f2"><span offset-key="4f021a9cc2b548248fa2bba736f267f2:0">The downside of the flexibility of var is that it can easily overwrite previously declared variables.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="5734e2df44ce4b72b189e45897aedb7e"><span offset-key="5734e2df44ce4b72b189e45897aedb7e:0">The block-scope limitations of let and const were introduced to easily avoid accidentally overwriting variable values.</span></span>

<span key="7b268d93d3ae4e499300d47d1fc6c786">**Global Variables**</span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="decd03097dd9401a9754305e128644b0"><span offset-key="decd03097dd9401a9754305e128644b0:0">Any variables declared without a declaration term will be considered </span>**`global scope`**<span offset-key="decd03097dd9401a9754305e128644b0:2">.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="52221f9602a3474dbb8c3dc7f3bdc9a8"><span offset-key="52221f9602a3474dbb8c3dc7f3bdc9a8:0">Every time a variable is declared on the global scope, the change of collision increases.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="a8dfa2def7504eafa3f23c8ac5b27f10"><span offset-key="a8dfa2def7504eafa3f23c8ac5b27f10:0">Use the proper declarations to manage your code: Avoid being a sloppy programmer!</span></span>

## 

<span key="7078a3ed29ac47389924a3ae14faa782">**Closures**</span>

<span key="cb65c14e50cd4ce88af657fbc5a6947d">**Calculating Closures**</span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="9024563f616a454882cfa4aeea584945">**Closure**<span offset-key="9024563f616a454882cfa4aeea584945:1"> : The combination of a function and the lexical environment within which that function is declared.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="82adfa6ca0eb466b8f9de5be9262c202">**Use**<span offset-key="82adfa6ca0eb466b8f9de5be9262c202:1"> : A closure is when an inner function uses, or changes, variables in an outer function.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="5cc701414a094d9dac4dab258fbe4f47"><span offset-key="5cc701414a094d9dac4dab258fbe4f47:0">Very important for creativity, flexibility, and security of your code.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="aa1a6f4a00a04dd6ae0e6f04991dc229">**`Lexical Environment`**<span offset-key="aa1a6f4a00a04dd6ae0e6f04991dc229:1"> : Consists of any variables available within the scope in which a closure was declared (local inner, outer, and global).</span></span>

<span key="32bb647212c9452aad8a277002d63b43">**Closures and Scope**<span offset-key="32bb647212c9452aad8a277002d63b43:1"> Basic Closure Rules:</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="545f592fbebd4b60b9a63db17a594a86"><span offset-key="545f592fbebd4b60b9a63db17a594a86:0">Closures have access to all variables in it's lexical environment.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="0ef09ab4b3484c3fbbf15534756dfafd"><span offset-key="0ef09ab4b3484c3fbbf15534756dfafd:0">A closure will keep reference to all the variables when it was defined </span>**even if the outer function has returned**<span offset-key="0ef09ab4b3484c3fbbf15534756dfafd:2">.</span></span>

<span key="b92a44060b5340ee96e5dfde2c33be15">**Applications of Closures**</span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="1d9846a3b04e4cf382f97a1fa184bc60">**Private State**</span>

    -   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

        <span key="18bff6f3c18847ce8a24cf475386cdc4"><span offset-key="18bff6f3c18847ce8a24cf475386cdc4:0">JS does not have a way of declaring a function as exclusively private, however we can use closures to make a private state.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="d0924253e58440c4804c9c60c030ebbe">**Passing Arguments Implicitly**</span>

    -   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

        <span key="d3d5ad0709d04187ab6d5823dbf55437"><span offset-key="d3d5ad0709d04187ab6d5823dbf55437:0">We can use closures to pass down arguments to helper functions.</span></span>

    1

## 

<span key="4053e6fda861486a963cc5bf507212ec">**Context in Javascript**</span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="526247542351464a9879aa4590474620">**`Scope`**<span offset-key="526247542351464a9879aa4590474620:1"> : Refers to the visibility and availability of variables.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="e8103e5982dc4f53be222e25f47ae017">**`Context`**<span offset-key="e8103e5982dc4f53be222e25f47ae017:1"> : Refers to the value of the </span>**`this`**<span offset-key="e8103e5982dc4f53be222e25f47ae017:3"> keyword when code is executed.</span></span>

<span key="ef141188407c45e589883fd6856e4cf6">**What about** **`this`** **?**</span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="d4457b0045224e578beaff693c647476">**`This`**<span offset-key="d4457b0045224e578beaff693c647476:1"> : Keyword that exists in every function and evaluates to the object that is currently invoking that function.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="f4d846ae05bf41d49926bd5687d23ed8">**Method-Style Invocation**<span offset-key="f4d846ae05bf41d49926bd5687d23ed8:1"> : syntax goes like </span>`object.method(arg)`<span offset-key="f4d846ae05bf41d49926bd5687d23ed8:3">. (i.e. array.push, str.toUpperCase()</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="7247a765cfac4ab4ad7ffbdc5a393001">**`Context`**<span offset-key="7247a765cfac4ab4ad7ffbdc5a393001:1"> refers to the value of this within a function and </span>**`this`**<span offset-key="7247a765cfac4ab4ad7ffbdc5a393001:3"> refers to where a function is invoked.</span></span>

<span key="65811e2e2d224287b63d633225d02366">**Issues with Scope and Context**</span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="fd986a27dc2f410c8f8d48c935986a06"><span offset-key="fd986a27dc2f410c8f8d48c935986a06:0">If </span>`this`<span offset-key="fd986a27dc2f410c8f8d48c935986a06:2"> is called using normal function style invocation, our output will be the contents of the global object.</span></span>

<span key="8caf5b6e53dc4e7185c9391211bc66cc">**When Methods have an Unexpected Context**</span>

1

<span key="a64a80c01bd84f63bedb1d1b7e8e2f92">**Strictly Protecting the Global Object**</span>

<span key="c5825cf2628a4f0d9cf420b080a94a00"><span offset-key="c5825cf2628a4f0d9cf420b080a94a00:0">We can run JS in strict mode by tagging </span>`use strict`<span offset-key="c5825cf2628a4f0d9cf420b080a94a00:2"> at the top of our program.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="6dd41323bc9c4bc98698c2752cde668a"><span offset-key="6dd41323bc9c4bc98698c2752cde668a:0">If we try to invoke this on our global function in strict mode we will no longer be able to access it and instead just get undefined.</span></span>

<span key="a72208ca81054621944c56f1ad24485b">**Changing Context using Bind**</span>

<span key="567c6878189040589474a007095784e3"><span offset-key="567c6878189040589474a007095784e3:0">"The simplest use of </span>**`bind()`**<span offset-key="567c6878189040589474a007095784e3:2"> is to make a function that, no matter how it is called, is called with a particular this value".</span></span>

## 

<span key="43bfa0cda0f449879e4dfd340dab3e91">**Arrow Functions aka Fat Arrows**</span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="4f4353aedb8f4a528c121ed3d63f02f2">**`=>`**<span offset-key="4f4353aedb8f4a528c121ed3d63f02f2:1"> : A more concise way of declaring a function and also considers the behavior of </span>`this`<span offset-key="4f4353aedb8f4a528c121ed3d63f02f2:3"> and context.</span></span>

<span key="ba74f58422204d9197e86221a1578dda">**Anatomy of an Arrow Function**</span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="9a1aa3998b0e4c7ea013c12931dca9fa"><span offset-key="9a1aa3998b0e4c7ea013c12931dca9fa:0">If there is only a single parameter there is no need to add parenthesis before the arrow function.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="adfdd91b01c54ec1a9440aee481ade15"><span offset-key="adfdd91b01c54ec1a9440aee481ade15:0">However if there are zero parameters then you must add an empty set of parentheses.</span></span>

<span key="a9deac77512e4ec5a169d0be05cc3e08">**Single Expression Arrow Functions**</span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="153b70a905d14c7797a9af19c9ee584d"><span offset-key="153b70a905d14c7797a9af19c9ee584d:0">Arrow functions, </span>*unlike*<span offset-key="153b70a905d14c7797a9af19c9ee584d:2"> normal functions, carry over context, binding </span>`this`<span offset-key="153b70a905d14c7797a9af19c9ee584d:4"> lexically.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="4046ea4311a14a79b47ce677945bbdd9"><span offset-key="4046ea4311a14a79b47ce677945bbdd9:0">Value of </span>`this`<span offset-key="4046ea4311a14a79b47ce677945bbdd9:2"> inside an arrow function is not dependent on how it is invoked.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="83ebb732cf484d3982bad98b451545d9"><span offset-key="83ebb732cf484d3982bad98b451545d9:0">Because arrow functions already have a </span>*bound context*<span offset-key="83ebb732cf484d3982bad98b451545d9:2">, you can't reassign </span>`this`<span offset-key="83ebb732cf484d3982bad98b451545d9:4">.</span></span>

<a href="review-of-previous-concepts.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1awozwy r-14lw9ot r-190qawg r-z2wwpe r-rs99b7 r-4dj0k7 r-1loqt21 r-1quu1zo r-1ro0kt6 r-18u37iz r-16y2uox r-1wbh5a2 r-nsbfu8 r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"></a>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMjQgMjQiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHN0cm9rZT0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIiBzdHJva2Utd2lkdGg9IjIiIHN0cm9rZS1saW5lY2FwPSJyb3VuZCIgc3Ryb2tlLWxpbmVqb2luPSJyb3VuZCIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgZGF0YS1ybnctaW50LWNsYXNzPSJuZWFyZXN0X18yNTctNzI3MzNfXyIgY2xhc3M9InItMXJhc2kzaCByLTE0NzJtd2cgci0xdnppOHhpIHItbHJzbGxwIj48cGF0aCBkPSJNMTkgMTJINU0xMiAxOWwtNy03IDctNyI+PC9wYXRoPjwvc3ZnPg==" class="r-1rasi3h r-1472mwg r-1vzi8xi r-lrsllp" />

<a href="reiew.html#arrow-functions-aka-fat-arrows" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-855088 r-dwliz8 r-1loqt21 r-18u37iz r-lqms97 r-dnmrzs r-iphfwy r-1guathk r-1h8ys4a r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr r-7xmw5f"></a>

Arrow Functions aka Fat Arrows
